@3080ti_US EVGA Queue notify: General availability for GeForce RTX 3080 Ti begins June 3rd. For the US/EU EVGA.com stores, EVGA Elite members will have 24hr exclusive access beginning June 3 at 6AM PDT / 3PM CEST to sign up for an EVGA GeForce RTX 3080 Ti via the auto-notify queue on their respective EVGA.com store. Non-Elite members may begin to enter the auto-notify queue June 4 at approximately 6AM PDT / 3PM CEST on their respective EVGA.com store.
 
General availability for GeForce RTX 3070 Ti begins June 10th. For the US/EU EVGA.com stores, EVGA Elite members will have 24hr exclusive access beginning June 10 at 6AM PDT / 3PM CEST to sign up for an EVGA GeForce RTX 3070 Ti via the auto-notify queue on their respective EVGA.com store. Non-Elite members may begin to enter the auto-notify queue June 11 at approximately 6AM PDT / 3PM CEST on their respective EVGA.com store. https://forums.evga.com//Introducing-the-EVGA-GeForce-RTX-3080-Ti-RTX-3070-Ti-Series-Graphics-Cards-m3318858.aspx
